name:K‍a‍z‍z‍y‍ ‍t‍r‍a‍v‍e‍l‍e‍r
info:Business 2-bed Room
info:Stayed in July 2023
info:Business travelers
info:4 Reviews
rating:4
posted:Posted July 17, 2023
msg:Inspirok Hotel Tongxiang- First time back in Tongxiang after 4 years.  7 nights in a spacious "Business Room" in building B with 2 very firm king single beds that gave me a sore upper back. (I don't have back problems normally...) Flat pillows.  The hopeless Air-conditioning struggled to get to an absolute low of 23C and was noisy. (32C days and 26C nights.). Huge bathroom with bath. Flow limited shower with hand shower and rain shower.  Mostly quiet due to reduced occupancy and outside traffic.  Good blockout curtains. International power points with USB power but you must have an earth pin if you want to use an Aussie plug. (Or risk manually pushing up the earth lockout.)  Many free english movies available now on the tv in reasonable quality.  One thing that I found particularly handy was that a small tube of liquid laundry detergent is supplied and some hooks above the bath.

There was no bar fridge in my room on arrival but one was quickly supplied, gratis, when I asked. (Empty).

Large shopping mall one block from the hotel and small 7-eleven type shop very near the front entrance where you can buy tsing taos for 6rmb.

The included buffet breakfast was pretty average with fewer choices and poorer quality than similar 5* hotels.  Very average automatic coffee machines and coffee pots. It was also so overcrowded on the Sunday- with a convention booking- that many people could not be seated.  Most mornings it was reasonably quiet. 

Excellent room service Indonesian fried rice.  I also had the "all you can eat" buffet a couple of nights but thought that it was over priced for the quality of food available at 138RMB (approx 30aud.)

Reasonable wifi access throughout the hotel and I was able to read my Gmail but not send it.  (I couldn't even download it in Jiangsu.)  

There is no option on the Trip booking page to ask for 'special requests" for this hotel.  Also no option to ask for a non smoking floor and I wasn't asked at check-in.  Very annoying.
----------------------------------------

There are 6 bottles of water in the room, and disposable items are all at a cost, not that cheap. Regardless of the personnel in the guest room or the restaurant, their service awareness exceeds that of Shanghai's government reception hotels.

2）致電房務中心，告知有一次性浴缸套，並且很快送來房間了

5）早餐的山東煎餅很好吃
6）免費礦泉水每天有6-8瓶，喝完還能要求補，態度很好👍

posted:Posted February 18, 2024
msg:桐鄉振石大酒店是當地最好的五星級酒店，我每次回老家桐鄉基本上住這個酒店，去年的“桐鄉發展大會”也在這裏召開。過年期間客房基本上是滿的，早餐還比較豐富，酒店環境也非常好，很多旅客在酒店花園裡拍照留念。出行比較方便，停車位比較多，登記車牌號出入自動免費。我訂的“商務雙人間”也升級了“豪華雙人間”，比較人性化。但與剛開業的時候相比，早餐遜色了不少，不夠豐盛，小麪、餛飩及豆花連可口的湯料都沒有，食之無味，水果也不豐富，希望酒店在早餐方面下點功夫，這樣才能吸引更多的旅客。

次回も利用したい。
